to this Privacy Policy or other communications with you; and</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">Offline business interactions you have with us, such as

in accordance with this Privacy Policy.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">“<b>Personal Data</b>” means any information about an individual from which

affiliates, you or others. </p></div></li></ul></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>In connection with a sale or business transaction.</b></p></div><ul><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">We have a legitimate interest in disclosing or transferring your

portion of our business, assets, or shares (including in connection with any
bankruptcy or similar proceedings).<i> </i>
</p></div></li></ul></li></ul><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>CHOICES </b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">We strive to provide you with choices under applicable law regarding certain Personal Data uses, particularly around marketing and advertising. </p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">You may opt out from:</p></div><ul><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">Receiving marketing-related emails from us. </p></div></li></ul><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">We will try to respond to you as soon as reasonably practicable. These companies place or recognise a unique cookie on your browser (including through the use of pixel tags).  They also use these technologies, along with information they collect about your online use, to recognise you
across the devices you use, such as a mobile phone and a laptop.  If you would like more information about this practice, and to learn how to opt out of it in desktop and mobile browsers on the particular device on which you are accessing this Privacy Policy, please
visit <a data-utid="link" href="http://optout.aboutads.info/" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank">http://optout.aboutads.info/#/</a> and <a data-utid="link" href="http://optout.networkadvertising.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank">http://optout.networkadvertising.org/#/</a>. apps.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>COOKIES AND OTHER INFORMATION </b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">For further information on how we use cookies and other information, please consult our <a data-utid="link" href="https://www.axora.com/cookie-policy" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_self">cookie policy</a>. </p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>TRANSFERS</b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">Your Personal Data may be stored and processed in any country where we have facilities or in which we engage service providers, and by using the Services you understand that your Personal Data will be transferred to countries outside of your country of residence, which may have data protection rules that are different from those of your country.  In certain circumstances, courts, law enforcement agencies, regulatory agencies or security authorities in those other countries may be entitled to access your Personal Data.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">Some non-European Economic Area (EEA) countries are recognised by the European Commission as providing an adequate level of data protection according to EEA standards (the full list of these countries is available here:  <a data-utid="link" href="https://protect-us.mimecast.com/s/oCgSCkROBgiN8vL8H84n-A" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank">https://ec.europa.eu/info/law/law-topic/data-protection/data-transfers-outside-eu/adequacy-protection-personal-data-non-eu-countries_en</a>). For transfers from the EEA to countries not considered adequate by the European Commission, we have put in place adequate measures, such as standard contractual clauses adopted by the European Commission to protect your Personal Data. You may obtain a copy of these measures by contacting us at <a data-utid="link" href="mailto:legal@axora.com" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank">legal@axora.com</a>.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>SECURITY</b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">The security of your Personal Data important to us. We have put in place a number of appropriate organisational, technical and physical security measures designed to protect the Personal Data within our organisation. Unfortunately, no data transmission or storage system can be guaranteed to be 100% secure.  If you have reason to believe that your interaction with us is no longer secure, please immediately notify us in accordance with the <a data-utid="link" href="https://www.axora.com/contact" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_self">Contact us</a> section below.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>RETENTION</b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">We retain Personal Data only as long as needed or permitted in light of the purposes for which they were obtained and consistent with applicable law, regulatory, tax, accounting or reporting requirements. To determine the appropriate retention period for Personal Data,
we consider:
</p></div><ul><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">The nature of the personal data.</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">The length of time during which we have an ongoing
relationship with you and provide the Services to you (for example, for as long
as you have an account with us or keep using the Services).</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">      
Whether there is a legal obligation to which we are subject
(for example, certain laws require us to keep records of transactions for a
certain period of time before we can delete them).</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">      
Whether retention is advisable in light of our legal position
(such as in regard to applicable statutes of limitations, litigation or
regulatory investigations).  </p></div></li></ul><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>YOUR RIGHTS</b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">You may be entitled under applicable law to request to exercise the following rights: </p></div><ul><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>Access and correction </b>
Request access to, and a copy of your Personal
Data from us. You can also request that any incorrect or incomplete Personal Data
that we hold about you are corrected, though we may need to verify the accuracy
of the new data you provide to us for example.</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>Restriction
</b>Request that we that we interrupt the processing of Personal Data under certain conditions.
</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>Deletion
</b>Request the deletion of your Personal Data stored by us under certain conditions. Please note that we may need to retain certain Personal Data for recordkeeping purposes and/or to complete any transactions that you began prior to requesting a change or deletion.
</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>Portability
</b>Request a portable copy of your Personal Data for the purpose of transferring it to another company. 
</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>Object
</b>Object to processing of your Personal Data or withdraw your consent under certain conditions. 
</p></div></li><li><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b> Right to complain to supervisory authority
</b>Make a complaint with the competent supervisory authority for your country. The competent supervisory authority in the UK for data protection issues is the Information Commissioner's Office (ICO) (<a data-utid="link" href="http://www.ico.org.uk/" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank">www.ico.org.uk</a><i>)</i>. If you would like to request the exercise of any of the above rights where available to you under applicable law, you may email us at legal@axora.com.We will respond to your request consistent with applicable law.  For your protection, we may only implement requests with respect to the Personal Data associated with the particular email address that you use to send us your request, and we may need to verify your identity before implementing your request. We will try to respond to your request as soon as reasonably practicable.</p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]"><b>WEBSITES WE LINK TO</b></p></div><div class="MuiGrid-root MuiGrid-container MuiGrid-item MuiGrid-align-items-xs-center"><p as="p" style="white-space:no-wrap;color:#222838;text-align:;font-size:17px;font-weight:normal;line-height:32px" variant="[object Object]">This Privacy Policy does not address, and we are not responsible for, the privacy, information, or other practices of any third parties, including any third party operating any website or service to which the Services link, such as social media websites.
